CREATE TABLE gstform5esubmissiondetails (
  id varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  dtperiodstart  date DEFAULT NULL,
  dtperiodend  date DEFAULT NULL,
  status int(2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  response  varchar(2048) DEFAULT "",
  responsecode varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
  esubmissiondate date DEFAULT NULL,
  esubmissionjson mediumtext,
  messagecode varchar(255) DEFAULT "",	
  entity varchar(255) DEFAULT "",  
  company varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `gstform5esubmission_fk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Dipak Dorkar 18th July 2018
# DBS Integration - Bank Account mapping table 

CREATE TABLE bankaccountcoamapping (
  id VARCHAR (255),
  bankid  VARCHAR (63),
  bankaccountname VARCHAR(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
  bankaccountnumber  VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  bankaccountdetails longtext NOT NULL ,
  company VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  deskeraaccount VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company (companyid),
  FOREIGN KEY (deskeraaccount) REFERENCES account (id)
) ENGINE = INNODB DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8;

#Bhakti Chavare 18th July 2018
create table passwordpolicy(policyid varchar(255) NOT NULL,
companyid varchar(255) NOT NULL,
minchar int(5) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
maxchar int(5) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
minnum int(5) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
minalphabet int(5) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
specialchar tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
defpass varchar(60) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
ppass varchar(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
setpolicy tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
PRIMARY KEY (policyid),
KEY companyid (companyid),
CONSTRAINT fk_policy_company FOREIGN KEY (companyid) REFERENCES company(companyid)) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Dipak Dorkar 20th July 2018
drop table bankaccountcoamapping;

CREATE TABLE bankaccountcoamapping (
  id VARCHAR (255) NOT NULL,
  bankid  VARCHAR (63),
  bankaccountname VARCHAR(255)  DEFAULT NULL,
  bankaccountnumber  VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  bankaccountdetails longtext NOT NULL ,
  company VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company (companyid),
  FOREIGN KEY (id) REFERENCES account (id)
) ENGINE = INNODB DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8;

#Aman Shah 20th July 2018

CREATE TABLE gsttransactionlistingsubmissiondetails (
  id varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  identifier varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  totalchunk int(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  currentchunk int(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  taxrefno  varchar(20) DEFAULT "",
  gstregno  varchar(20) DEFAULT "",
  dtperiodstart  date DEFAULT NULL,
  dtperiodend  date DEFAULT NULL,
  dtiafcreation  date DEFAULT NULL,
  iafversion  varchar(20) DEFAULT "",
  chunkresponsedatetime datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  requestpayload mediumtext,
  status int(2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  responsecode varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
  messagecode varchar(255) DEFAULT "",
  responsepayload mediumtext,
  company varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `gsttransactionlistingsubmissiondetails_fk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

create table integrationparty (
id smallint(6) not NULL,
integrationpartyname varchar(255),
integrationpartyhiddenname varchar(255),
integrationconfig text,
integrationglobalsettings text,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
insert into integrationparty VALUES (1, 'UPS', 'upsIntegration', NULL, NULL);
insert into integrationparty VALUES (2, 'Avalara', 'avalaraIntegration', NULL, NULL);
insert into integrationparty VALUES (7, 'IRAS', 'irasIntegration', NULL, NULL);

create table integrationpartycountrymapping (
id varchar(63) not null,
integrationparty smallint(6),
country varchar(255) not null,
PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
FOREIGN KEY (`integrationparty`) REFERENCES `integrationparty` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
FOREIGN KEY (`country`) REFERENCES `country` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
